Coiled Tubing Built to Revolutionize the Industry</h2><p>Patented single-layer steel armouring for the world&#x27;s most demanding installations.</p><p>Power grids, telecommunications backbones, transport networks, industrial sites, geothermal wells, and oil and gas operations share one challenge: the cables and conduits underpinning them must survive sabotage, environmental degradation, mechanical stress, and chemical attack — for decades — without failing.</p><p>Conventional armoured cables and coiled tubing fail in predictable ways: bird-nesting under compression, kinking under bending, corrosion in harsh environments, vulnerability to physical attack. ARCAB&#x27;s patented technology eliminates these failure modes through a fundamental redesign of how the armour is constructed.</p><h2 id="a-new-generation-of-armoured-cable-and-coiled-tubing" tabindex="0">A new generation of armoured cable and coiled tubing</h2><p>Our single-layer steel armour is built from interlocking high-strength profiles. The result is a cable or tube that is torsionally balanced, structurally stable when bent, semi-rigid and pushable into long horizontal runs, smooth and low-friction, gas-tight and impermeable, and chemically resistant to H₂S, ammonia, sulphuric acid, and saltwater.</p><p>It is the first armouring technology that combines the strength of solid steel with the flexibility of a wound cable — what we call controlled flexibility.</p><h2 id="three-application-domains-where-the-difference-matters-most" tabindex="0">Three application domains where the difference matters most</h2><div class="block image align center next--is--slate is--first--of--block-type is--last--of--block-type previous--has--same--backgroundColor next--has--same--backgroundColor has--block-width--narrow has--background-color--default" style="--block-width:var(--narrow-container-width);--theme-color:#fff;--theme-high-contrast-color:#ecebeb;--theme-foreground-color:#000;--theme-low-contrast-foreground-color:#555555"><figure class="figure center large"><img class="responsive" src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1544955448-6346fb3cadc9?fm=jpg&amp;q=85&amp;w=2400&amp;auto=format&amp;fit=crop" loading="lazy" decoding="async" alt="Telecommunications tower at night" sizes="100vw"/></figure></div><h3 id="1-critical-infrastructure-security" tabindex="0">1. Critical infrastructure security</h3><p>Power grids, telecommunications, transport, and industrial sites face escalating threats: deliberate sabotage, geopolitical risk, vandalism, and accidental damage. The solid, gas-tight steel sheath provides physical protection that conventional cables cannot match. For network operators, utility owners, and critical-infrastructure operators, this is the difference between a vulnerability and a resilient asset.</p><div class="block image align center next--is--slate is--first--of--block-type is--last--of--block-type previous--has--same--backgroundColor next--has--same--backgroundColor has--block-width--narrow has--background-color--default" style="--block-width:var(--narrow-container-width);--theme-color:#fff;--theme-high-contrast-color:#ecebeb;--theme-foreground-color:#000;--theme-low-contrast-foreground-color:#555555"><figure class="figure center large"><img class="responsive" src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1759934553802-749f348a50b3?fm=jpg&amp;q=85&amp;w=2400&amp;auto=format&amp;fit=crop" loading="lazy" decoding="async" alt="Geothermal power plant with steam rising in mountain landscape" sizes="100vw"/></figure></div><h3 id="2-geothermal-heat-exchange" tabindex="0">2. Geothermal heat exchange</h3><p>Geothermal energy installations require coiled tubing that survives high pressure, high temperature, and aggressive ground chemistry over decades of service. Our high-stiffness, corrosion-resistant coiled tubing is engineered for exactly these conditions, supporting the global energy transition with infrastructure that lasts.</p><div class="block image align center next--is--slate is--first--of--block-type is--last--of--block-type previous--has--same--backgroundColor next--has--same--backgroundColor has--block-width--narrow has--background-color--default" style="--block-width:var(--narrow-container-width);--theme-color:#fff;--theme-high-contrast-color:#ecebeb;--theme-foreground-color:#000;--theme-low-contrast-foreground-color:#555555"><figure class="figure center large"><img class="responsive" src="https://images.unsplash.com/photo-1696059928249-f036c4d54338?fm=jpg&amp;q=85&amp;w=2400&amp;auto=format&amp;fit=crop" loading="lazy" decoding="async" alt="Oil drilling rig in remote desert landscape" sizes="100vw"/></figure></div><h3 id="3-oil-and-gas--the-heritage-application" tabindex="0">3. Oil and gas — the heritage application</h3><p>Well intervention, electric submersible pump (ESP) cables, downhole sensors, and fracking operations demand cable and tubing that withstand the most extreme environments on Earth. Our technology was originally developed for these conditions and has been refined through more than a decade of engineering work.</p><h2 id="patented-and-validated" tabindex="0">Patented and validated</h2><p>The technology is protected by four granted patents: three European patents (EP 3 007 178, EP 3 007 179, EP 3 006 801) and one German national patent (DE 10 2014 014 793 B4, granted January 2026). Material and electromagnetic properties have been validated in collaboration with Otto-von-Guericke University Magdeburg and the Fraunhofer Institute.</p></div></div></div></main></div><p id="route-announcer" role="alert" style="border:0;clip:rect(1px 1px 1px 1px);height:1px;margin:-1px;overflow:hidden;padding:0;position:absolute;width:1px;white-space:nowrap;word-wrap:normal"></p><footer id="footer"><div class="arcab-footer"><p class="arcab-footer__company">ARCAB</p><address class="arcab-footer__address">Hansavägen 13<br/>SE-245 65 Hjärup<br/>Sweden</address><a href="mailto:arcab@ljusa-tider.se" class="arcab-footer__email">arcab@ljusa-tider.se</a><p class="arcab-footer__colophon">armoured cables and coiled tubing</p></div></footer><div class="Toastify"></div></div><div role="complementary" aria-label="Sidebar" id="sidebar"></div><script charSet="UTF-8">window.__data={"router":{"location":{"pathname":"\u002Fen","search":"","hash":"","state":undefined,"key":"lhbjwx","query":{}},"action":"POP"},"intl":{"defaultLocale":"en","locale":"en","messages":{"Add link":"","An error has occurred while editing \"{name}\" field. armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."}]}],"styles":{},"plaintext":"Conventional armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation. Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals. ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."},"c1d3c0dd-a2ef-4b67-8893-c02398278eda":{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Farcab.ljusa-tider.se\u002Fstrand-bend-animation\u002F@@download\u002Ffile?ext=.mp4","size":"xl","@type":"video","align":"center","theme":"default","styles":{}},"dcfa9c45-26b0-4e58-8509-8616fe08599c":{"@type":"slate","theme":"default","value":[{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"The animation shows the priciple of ARCAB's interlocking strands gliding longitudinally as the cable bends (not to scale) — outer-arc strands stretching, inner-arc strands compressing. Conventional products are either fully rigid (like a solid pipe — strong but cannot be coiled, transported on a drum, or installed around bends) or fully flexible (like a standard electrical cable — coilable but cannot be pushed, deforms under load, and lacks structural integrity). simultaneously"},"ab673aa5-8ad7-41ea-a063-75447df985f5":{"@type":"title"},"b7a6aed8-ff3c-451c-b5eb-7cada17e7adc":{"@type":"slate","theme":"default","value":[{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"Conventional armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."}]}],"styles":{},"plaintext":"Conventional armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation. Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals. ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."},"c1d3c0dd-a2ef-4b67-8893-c02398278eda":{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Farcab.ljusa-tider.se\u002Fstrand-bend-animation\u002F@@download\u002Ffile?ext=.mp4","size":"xl","@type":"video","align":"center","theme":"default","styles":{}},"dcfa9c45-26b0-4e58-8509-8616fe08599c":{"@type":"slate","theme":"default","value":[{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"The animation shows the priciple of ARCAB's interlocking strands gliding longitudinally as the cable bends (not to scale) — outer-arc strands stretching, inner-arc strands compressing. Conventional products are either fully rigid (like a solid pipe — strong but cannot be coiled, transported on a drum, or installed around bends) or fully flexible (like a standard electrical cable — coilable but cannot be pushed, deforms under load, and lacks structural integrity). armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."}]}],"styles":{},"plaintext":"Conventional armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation. Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals. ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."},"c1d3c0dd-a2ef-4b67-8893-c02398278eda":{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Farcab.ljusa-tider.se\u002Fstrand-bend-animation\u002F@@download\u002Ffile?ext=.mp4","size":"xl","@type":"video","align":"center","theme":"default","styles":{}},"dcfa9c45-26b0-4e58-8509-8616fe08599c":{"@type":"slate","theme":"default","value":[{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"The animation shows the priciple of ARCAB's interlocking strands gliding longitudinally as the cable bends (not to scale) — outer-arc strands stretching, inner-arc strands compressing. ARCAB's interlocking armour is engineered to be flexible for installation and rigid for performance, simultaneously."}]}],"plaintext":"Controlled flexibility — the core innovation The fundamental design principle that enables all six properties is what we call controlled flexibility: the engineered balance between rigidity and bendability. Conventional products are either fully rigid (like a solid pipe — strong but cannot be coiled, transported on a drum, or installed around bends) or fully flexible (like a standard electrical cable — coilable but cannot be pushed, deforms under load, and lacks structural integrity). armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."}]}],"styles":{},"plaintext":"Conventional armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation. Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals. ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."},"c1d3c0dd-a2ef-4b67-8893-c02398278eda":{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Farcab.ljusa-tider.se\u002Fstrand-bend-animation\u002F@@download\u002Ffile?ext=.mp4","size":"xl","@type":"video","align":"center","theme":"default","styles":{}},"dcfa9c45-26b0-4e58-8509-8616fe08599c":{"@type":"slate","theme":"default","value":[{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"The animation shows the priciple of ARCAB's interlocking strands gliding longitudinally as the cable bends (not to scale) — outer-arc strands stretching, inner-arc strands compressing. armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."}]}],"styles":{},"plaintext":"Conventional armoured cables are built by helically winding multiple layers of steel wires or strips around an inner core. This produces a cable that is flexible enough to install but suffers from inherent torsional imbalance: the layers create competing internal stresses that, under compression or repeated handling, cause the wires to \"bird-nest\" — splaying outward and damaging both the armour and the inner core. Multi-layer designs also leave gaps that admit moisture and chemicals, and present uneven outer surfaces that increase friction during installation. Conventional coiled tubing has its own failure modes: kinking and ovalisation under bending, fatigue at the edges, and limited resistance to high pressure and aggressive chemicals. ARCAB's patented technology solves these problems together by replacing the multi-layer construction with a single-layer armouring built from interlocking high-strength steel profiles."},"c1d3c0dd-a2ef-4b67-8893-c02398278eda":{"url":"https:\u002F\u002Farcab.ljusa-tider.se\u002Fstrand-bend-animation\u002F@@download\u002Ffile?ext=.mp4","size":"xl","@type":"video","align":"center","theme":"default","styles":{}},"dcfa9c45-26b0-4e58-8509-8616fe08599c":{"@type":"slate","theme":"default","value":[{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"The animation shows the priciple of ARCAB's interlocking strands gliding longitudinally as the cable bends (not to scale) — outer-arc strands stretching, inner-arc strands compressing. ARCAB's interlocking armour is engineered to be flexible for installation and rigid for performance, simultaneously."}]}],"plaintext":"Controlled flexibility — the core innovation The fundamental design principle that enables all six properties is what we call controlled flexibility: the engineered balance between rigidity and bendability. Conventional products are either fully rigid (like a solid pipe — strong but cannot be coiled, transported on a drum, or installed around bends) or fully flexible (like a standard electrical cable — coilable but cannot be pushed, deforms under load, and lacks structural integrity). ARCAB's interlocking armour is engineered to be flexible for installation and rigid for performance, simultaneously."},"f4df1a8d-b399-424f-af17-49ba42a48faf":{"@type":"slate","value":[{"type":"h2","children":[{"text":"Patent portfolio"}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"The technology is protected by four granted patents from a single inventor partnership: Werner Führer and Werner Haberkamp, with priority date 10 October 2014."}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"EP 3 007 178 — High Rigidity Cable (European, granted)"}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"EP 3 007 179 — High Rigidity Cable and Method for Producing the Same (European, granted)"}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"EP 3 006 801 — \"Coiled-Tubing\"-Type Flexible Pipe and Production Method (European, granted)"}]},{"type":"p","children":[{"text":"DE 10 2014 014 793 B4 — Kabel hoher Steifigkeit und dessen Verwendung \u002F High-Stiffness Cable and Its Use (German national, granted January 2026)"}]}],"plaintext":"Patent portfolio The technology is protected by four granted patents from a single inventor partnership: Werner Führer and Werner Haberkamp, with priority date 10 October 2014. infrastructure that lasts: heat-exchange tubing must survive decades in environments combining high pressure, high temperature, aggressive ground water chemistry, and continuous thermal cycling. ARCAB's coiled tubing is engineered for exactly these conditions: high-temperature operation up to 280 °C in service (with material capability to +350 °C), chemical resistance to H₂S, ammonia, and sulphuric acid common in geothermal brines, pressure rating up to 450 bar for deep-well applications, single-layer interlocking armour that eliminates the seam-corrosion and weld-defect failure modes of conventional tubing, and a smooth interior for consistent fluid flow without scaling deposition at seams. The same coiled tubing serves heat-exchange systems for direct geothermal use, ground-source heat pump installations at industrial scale, and deep geothermal power generation."},"30123b39-f773-40b6-b34a-89650de8420f":{"@type":"slate","value":[{"type":"h2","children":[{"text":"2.
